вПЇ User approved Claude's plan
  вОњ ¬†Plan saved to: ~/.claude/plans/mighty-munching-yeti.md ¬Ј /plan to edit
     Vocabify: Fix 6 Issues Plan

     Context

     After the major refactor (SelectionPopover replacing TooltipBtn), several
     regressions and missing features surfaced:
     1. AI streaming shows no incremental updates (jumps from skeleton to final)
     2. VocabList has no edit capability
     3. Popover edit mode inputs can't receive focus
     4. VocabList and Popover use different theme rendering
     5. No unified theme control (options/content/popover out of sync)
     6. No tests covering these flows

     Issue 1: Streaming Not Incremental

     Root cause: isPartialEqual() in lib/aiService.ts only checks top-level key
     names and senses.length. When content grows within existing keys (e.g.,
     definition fills from "" to "a word..."), the check returns "equal" and
     suppresses the onPartial callback.

     Fix: Remove isPartialEqual entirely. Always call onPartial. React's virtual
      DOM diffing already prevents unnecessary DOM updates вАФ the equality gate
     is redundant and harmful.

     Files: lib/aiService.ts вАФ delete isPartialEqual method, always invoke
     options.onPartial(partial) inside the stream loop.

     Issue 2: VocabList Has No Edit

     Root cause: components/VocabList.tsx expanded view only has a delete
     button. No edit UI exists.

     Fix: Add an edit button to the expanded record row. When clicked, swap the
     read-only display for an inline edit form (same field structure as EditCard
      in SelectionPopover.tsx). Extract a shared RecordEditForm component to
     avoid duplication.

     Files:
     - components/VocabList.tsx вАФ add edit state, edit button, render
     RecordEditForm when editing
     - components/RecordEditForm.tsx (new) вАФ shared form extracted from
     SelectionPopover.tsx's EditCard
     - entrypoints/content/components/SelectionPopover.tsx вАФ refactor EditCard
     to use RecordEditForm

     Issue 3: Popover Edit Inputs Unfocusable

     Root cause: SelectionPopover.tsx line 128 has onMouseDown={(e) => 
     e.preventDefault()} on the popover container. This prevents the selection
     from being cleared when clicking the popover (which is desired in
     operation-bar/card mode), but it also blocks focus transfer to inputs in
     edit mode.

     Fix: Only preventDefault when the click target is NOT an interactive
     element:
     onMouseDown={(e) => {
       const tag = (e.target as HTMLElement).tagName
       if (tag !== 'INPUT' && tag !== 'TEXTAREA' && tag !== 'SELECT') {
         e.preventDefault()
       }
     }}

     Files: entrypoints/content/components/SelectionPopover.tsx

     Issues 4 & 5: Unified Theme System

     Root cause: Two independent localStorage keys exist:
     - Content script: 'vocabify-theme' (light/dark only, no system support)
     - Options/popup: 'vite-ui-theme' (light/dark/system)

     These never sync. The popover also hardcodes dark class (our earlier
     quick-fix) instead of respecting user preference.

     Fix: Create a single source of truth:
     1. Use one key: 'vocabify-theme' with values light | dark | system
     2. Create lib/theme.ts вАФ utility functions: getStoredTheme(),
     setStoredTheme(), resolveEffectiveTheme() (resolves 'system' to light/dark
     based on media query)
     3. Update theme-provider.tsx to use 'vocabify-theme' key
     4. Update content script resolveTheme() to support 'system' value
     5. Remove the hardcoded dark class from SelectionPopover вАФ it should
     inherit from the shadow root container
     6. Both options page and content script listen to storage events for live
     sync

     Files:
     - lib/theme.ts (new) вАФ shared theme utilities
     - components/custom/theme-provider.tsx вАФ use unified key
     - entrypoints/content/index.tsx вАФ use lib/theme.ts, handle 'system'
     - entrypoints/content/components/SelectionPopover.tsx вАФ remove hardcoded
     dark class

     Issue 6: Tests

     Add integration tests to tests/selection-ai-flow.spec.ts (existing file)
     covering:
     1. Streaming: Verify partial updates arrive before final (check that
     popover content changes incrementally)
     2. Popover edit: Select word вЖТ query вЖТ card вЖТ edit вЖТ type in input вЖТ save вЖТ
      verify record updated
     3. VocabList edit: Open sheet вЖТ expand record вЖТ edit вЖТ save вЖТ verify
     4. Theme sync: Set theme in options вЖТ verify content script container class
      updates

     These use the existing Playwright test infrastructure (WXT dev extension +
     fixture server pattern from the existing spec).

     Files: tests/selection-ai-flow.spec.ts

     Execution Order

     1. lib/theme.ts + theme-provider + content script theme (Issues 4 &¬†5) вАФ
     foundational, affects all UI
     2. SelectionPopover.tsx onMouseDown fix + remove hardcoded dark (Issues 3
     &¬†4)
     3. lib/aiService.ts streaming fix (Issue¬†1)
     4. components/RecordEditForm.tsx + VocabList edit + SelectionPopover
     refactor (Issue¬†2)
     5. Tests (Issue¬†6)

     Verification

     After implementation:
     1. pnpm run build passes
     2. Start dev server, load extension in browser
     3. Select text вЖТ operation-bar appears (themed correctly per user
     preference)
     4. Click query вЖТ card shows streaming updates (definition fills character
     by character)
     5. Click edit вЖТ inputs are focusable and typeable
     6. Save вЖТ record updates
     7. Open VocabList sheet вЖТ expand record вЖТ edit вЖТ save вЖТ verify
     8. Open options вЖТ change theme вЖТ popover and wordlist update immediately
     9. Run pnpm test вАФ all specs pass

вПЇ User approved Claude's plan
  вОњ ¬†Plan saved to: ~/.claude/plans/mighty-munching-yeti.md ¬Ј /plan to edit
     Simplify SelectionPopover: Replace Custom Positioning with shadcn Popover

     Context

     The current SelectionPopover uses:
     1. Manual viewport-clamped coordinate calculation (getViewportBounds,
     clamp, safeLeft/safeTop)
     2. A useLayoutEffect measurement loop for height
     3. Global functions (window.__vocabifyShowOperationBar,
     __vocabifyShowSavedCard, __vocabifyDismissSelectionAction) for
     communication between DOM listeners and React state
     4. A hoverBridge with 220ms delay timer for hover dismiss

     User wants all of this removed вАФ use shadcn Popover with a virtual anchor,
     React state drives open/close directly, no timers.

     Approach

     Architecture

     entrypoints/content/index.tsx (InPageUIRoot)
     вФЬвФАвФА React state: popoverState (null | { rect, mode, ... })
     вФЬвФАвФА useEffect: DOM listeners (mouseup, mousedown, keydown) set state
     directly
     вФЬвФАвФА Popover (shadcn, controlled: open={!!popoverState})
     вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА PopoverAnchor: invisible fixed div positioned at selection rect
     вФВ   вФФвФАвФА PopoverContent: renders OperationBar / Card / Edit based on mode
     вФФвФАвФА InPageUI (wordlist sheet, unchanged)

     Key change: no global functions, no hoverBridge, no custom positioning 
     math. Radix's floating-ui handles viewport collision/flip automatically.

     Virtual Anchor Pattern

     // Invisible anchor positioned at the selection rect
     <PopoverAnchor asChild>
       <div
         style={{
           position: 'fixed',
           left: popoverState.rect.left,
           top: popoverState.rect.top,
           width: popoverState.rect.width,
           height: popoverState.rect.height,
           pointerEvents: 'none',
         }}
       />
     </PopoverAnchor>

     Radix positions PopoverContent relative to this anchor using side,
     sideOffset, align, and built-in collision detection.

     Simplified Open/Close Logic

     - mouseup вЖТ set popoverState (operation-bar or saved-card)
     - mousedown outside вЖТ set popoverState = null
     - Escape вЖТ set popoverState = null
     - Hover on highlighted word вЖТ set popoverState (card)
     - Pointer leaves popover вЖТ set popoverState = null (immediate, no timer)
     - onInteractOutside (Radix built-in) вЖТ close

     PopoverContent Portal

     Important: must portal into shadow DOM, not document.body. Use Radix's
     container prop:
     <PopoverPrimitive.Portal container={shadowRootContainer}>

     Files to Modify

     1. entrypoints/content/index.tsx вАФ Remove: hoverBridge, global __vocabify*
     functions, custom getSelectionActionPlacement, getUsableSelectionRect (keep
      the rect getter but simplify). DOM listeners directly call
     setPopoverState.
     2. entrypoints/content/components/SelectionPopover.tsx вАФ Rewrite: remove
     all positioning logic (getViewportBounds, clamp, safeLeft, safeTop,
     measuredHeight, useLayoutEffect, SELECTION_POPOVER_ESTIMATED_HEIGHT). Use
     shadcn Popover + PopoverAnchor + PopoverContent with side="top",
     sideOffset={8}, collisionPadding={12}.
     3. components/ui/popover.tsx вАФ Minor: add container prop passthrough to
     Portal for shadow DOM rendering.

     What Stays

     - The content inside the popover (OperationBar, Card, EditCard,
     SavedFooter) вАФ unchanged
     - The useAIStream hook вАФ unchanged
     - Event logic (what triggers what mode) вАФ same, just expressed as direct
     state sets

     Verification

     1. pnpm run build passes
     2. Select text вЖТ popover appears above/below selection (Radix auto-flips)
     3. Click query вЖТ card mode with streaming
     4. Hover saved word вЖТ card appears immediately, leaves immediately on
     pointer exit
     5. Escape dismisses
     6. Click outside dismisses
     7. Edit mode inputs are focusable
     8. Popover stays within viewport on edge selections

  еТМ content/index.tsxгАВ

      350 +function extractSourceContext(range: Range): string {         
      351 +  let node: Node | null = range.commonAncestorContainer       
      352 +  while (node && node.nodeType !== Node.ELEMENT_NODE) node = n
          +ode.parentNode                                                
      353 +  const block = node as HTMLElement | null                    
      354 +  if (!block) return range.toString().trim()                  
      355 +  const full = block.textContent || ''                        
      356 +  const sel = range.toString().trim()                         
      357 +  if (!sel) return full.slice(0, 240).trim()                  
      358 +  const idx = full.indexOf(sel)                               
      359 +  if (idx === -1) return full.slice(0, 240).trim()            
      360 +  const start = Math.max(0, idx - 100)                        
      361 +  const end = Math.min(full.length, idx + sel.length + 100)   
      362 +  return full.slice(start, end).trim()                        
      363 +}

          +SELECTION_CONTAINER),

      373 +  if (delta < 0) return `${delta}`                            
      374 +  return '¬±0'                                                 
      375 +}

вПЇ User approved Claude's plan
  вОњ ¬†Plan saved to: ~/.claude/plans/mighty-munching-yeti.md ¬Ј /plan to edit
     Polish SelectionPopover: Streaming UX + Visual Refinement

     Context

     Current issues:
     1. Streaming granularity: partialJson.ts only emits when strings/values
     complete, not mid-word. User sees large jumps (term appears, then all
     senses at once) instead of smooth token-by-token flow.
     2. Width flicker: Popover uses w-auto min-w-[200px] max-w-[320px], so it
     resizes during streaming causing position shifts.
     3. Border quality: border-white/8 with soft shadow 0 4px 12px 
     rgba(0,0,0,0.15) lacks definition. Per CLAUDE.md/global.css design
     principle: "1px borders instead of shadows" for engineered aesthetic
     (Raycast/Linear/Obsidian).
     4. No visual verification loop: Need to screenshot and iterate.

     Approach

     1. Streaming Granularity: Token-Level Display

     Problem: partialJson.ts discards incomplete strings. For {"term":"hel, it
     returns {} until the closing ".

     Solution A (Preferred): Capture raw buffer increments and display them in a
      "streaming preview" zone before schema validation.

     Solution B: Modify parsePartialJson to return in-progress string values via
      a raw field:
     return { partial: parsed, complete, raw: { term: 'hel', definition: 'A 
     proc...' } }

     Decision: Use Solution A вАФ less invasive, keeps parser pure. Add a
     streamingText state in useAIStream that shows the tail of the raw buffer
     (last 100 chars) until onPartial emits a structured update.

     2. Fixed Popover Width

     Replace w-auto with fixed width stages:
     - Operation bar: w-[260px] (narrow, action-focused)
     - Card mode: w-[340px] (reading-optimized, matches VocabList expanded
     width)
     - Edit mode: w-[380px] (form fields need room)

     This prevents layout shift and matches CLAUDE.md principle: "Information
     density > decorative space."

     3. Border Refinement

     Current:
     border-white/8 bg-popover shadow-[0_4px_12px_rgba(0,0,0,0.15)]

     Target (per global.css design):
     border-white/12 bg-surface-2 shadow-none

     Rationale:
     - Increase border alpha from 0.08 to 0.12 (more visible but still subtle)
     - Use --surface-2 (#323234) instead of --popover for elevation separation
     - Remove soft shadow, rely on border for structure (Raycast/Linear
     aesthetic)
     - Add inner glow for depth: ring-1 ring-inset ring-white/4

     4. Visual Verification Loop

     After each change:
     1. Screenshot with mcp__playwright__browser_take_screenshot
     2. Read image to verify border clarity, shadow removal, width consistency
     3. Iterate until it matches Raycast/Obsidian professional tool aesthetic

     Files to Modify

     1. entrypoints/content/useAIStream.ts (new or extend existing) вАФ Add
     rawBuffer state that accumulates all chunks. Expose streamingText (tail of
     buffer) alongside partial.
     2. entrypoints/content/components/SelectionPopover.tsx вАФ
       - Replace w-auto with fixed widths per mode
       - Update className: border-white/12 bg-surface-2 shadow-none ring-1 
     ring-inset ring-white/4
       - In Card skeleton/loading state, show streamingText as fading preview
     text before structured fields appear
     3. assets/global.css (if needed) вАФ Verify --surface-2 variable exists for
     dark mode

     Verification Steps

     1. Build: pnpm run build
     2. Select text вЖТ operation bar appears (verify 260px width, border
     visibility)
     3. Click query вЖТ card mode streaming:
       - Verify fixed 340px width (no resize)
       - Verify token-level text preview appears before term/phonetic populate
       - Screenshot before/after senses load вАФ no layout shift
     4. Visual: Screenshot and compare border thickness, shadow removal, surface
      contrast
     5. Edit mode: Verify 380px width, inputs focusable

     Success Criteria

     - Streaming feels smooth (token-level preview, then structured fields)
     - Popover width never changes during streaming
     - Border is crisp and visible (white/12 alpha, no shadow)
     - Aesthetic matches Raycast/Linear (engineered, not decorative)
     - Screenshot shows clear visual separation from page background
